  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d321cfd1-71e4-4932-9588-5efebf2c132c'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText8429843303693721987" style="display:none"><b><i>#1 Bestseller in Superhero Fiction! <br />Available in paperback, Kindle, and Kindle Unlimited!</i><br /><br />From Bestselling &amp; Award-Winning author Ammar Habib comes this story of vigilante justice! </b><br /><br />For the past four years, everyone thought Ethan Daniels was dead and gone. But now he is back with a vengeance. After the gruesome death of his adopted sister at the hands of a merciless gang, there is nothing he wants more than revenge. He can't sleep. He can't think. All he hears are her cries and all he sees is her death. Ethan comes home to take on one of the world’s most notorious crime lords in his bid for revenge. Using his vast resources, advanced skills, and an arsenal of weaponry, Ethan dons the mask of a vigilante and wages a one-man-war against the crime lord’s empire. However, he doesn't expect a reunion with Katrina, the girl he loved as a boy. After multiple reencounters with her, Ethan's resolve begins to waver as he is forced to realize that he can't have both love and vengeance. Retribution exacts a price while fate—well, she has plans of her own.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3069948882" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12845867273649033998">It starts off like a typical superhero origin with a bit of mystery surrounding Ethan's past. However, as things are unraveled, the story gets its own unique features. Ethan's personal journey is the main focus of the story, and the plot takes a back seat to his character arc. Katrina and William offers good foils to his character but in different ways. I like how the story focuses more on the hero than the villain, something not seen in most modern superhero tales. That being said, the action s</span>
  <span id="freeText12845867273649033998" style="display:none">It starts off like a typical superhero origin with a bit of mystery surrounding Ethan's past. However, as things are unraveled, the story gets its own unique features. Ethan's personal journey is the main focus of the story, and the plot takes a back seat to his character arc. Katrina and William offers good foils to his character but in different ways. I like how the story focuses more on the hero than the villain, something not seen in most modern superhero tales. That being said, the action scenes are great! They are very detailed, and I could see them being scenes straight out of a movie. A well earned 4.5 stars from me. </span>

<div id="review_2457931992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2457931992" />
    <a title="Shelle Perry" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47890275-shelle-perry"><img alt="Shelle Perry" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599701277p2/47890275.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2457931992?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelle Perry" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelle Perry" href="/user/show/47890275-shelle-perry">Shelle Perry</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47890275-shelle-perry?shelf=blogged-about">blogged-about</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47890275-shelle-perry?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2457931992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15947584311325498152">As origin stories go this was pretty good. Ethan Daniels is a bad ass superhero of a questionable supernatural origin. He is fighting government corruption while trying to live a normal life and protect those he loves. He is troubled and flawed and not quite sure if his hellbent quest for vengeance is what he should be doing with his life. So, it is also a bit of a cliche. Unfortunately, it didn’t help much that every time he dispatched a bad guy he sounded like Oliver Queen uttering his famous </span>
  <span id="freeText15947584311325498152" style="display:none">As origin stories go this was pretty good. Ethan Daniels is a bad ass superhero of a questionable supernatural origin. He is fighting government corruption while trying to live a normal life and protect those he loves. He is troubled and flawed and not quite sure if his hellbent quest for vengeance is what he should be doing with his life. So, it is also a bit of a cliche. Unfortunately, it didn’t help much that every time he dispatched a bad guy he sounded like Oliver Queen uttering his famous “You have failed this city!”. Call it an homage to great graphic novel super- and anti-superheroes.<br /><br />The book could have used another edit for grammar and spelling, but there is so much that is good about it. The author has built a world with a political climate that is not as far off in this country as we would like to believe, where basic constitutional rights have been revoked and citizens are pretty much on their own. It surely seems to be a social commentary, but plays out well in the framework of the story. It allows the characters to walk a fine line between perpetrating injustice and just not doing anything about it<br /><br />While Ethan’s backstory might be a bit on the predictable side, it is populated with great and at times complex characters. Katrina, William, and, surprisingly, David are exceptional standouts. If you know a man by those who love him, then we know a great deal about our protagonist. Ethan is accessible as a character even knowing almost nothing about him up front and the bits and pieces told in flashback were a great way to catch the reader up.<br /><br />This is an action tale where exposition doesn’t take a back seat to the high octane fight scenes which read more like a movie than a book. There is enough suspense, with a fair share of twists to keep the reader fully engaged from cover to cover and it was certainly not a chore for me to finish this all in one sitting.<br /><br />With a little polish this could be a five-star read, but even so, the story is strong enough to make me want to read the next books in the series. Ethan Daniels and his alter ego have some serious potential.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15947584311325498152" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carla" href="/user/show/23107654-carla">Carla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22916648-dark-guardian">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1422113790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8203114041006103768">*I was given a copy of this book as a gift from Stephanie's Book Reports in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>After not hearing from Ethan Daniels for four long years, his loved one presumes he is dead. Needless to say, everyone is shocked by his sudden return. After spending time with him, some people soon notice that Ethan is not the same man who vanished all those years ago. After witnessing the gruesome death of his adopted sister, Naira, he wants one thing-revenge. He returns home to take out t</span>
  <span id="freeText8203114041006103768" style="display:none">*I was given a copy of this book as a gift from Stephanie's Book Reports in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />After not hearing from Ethan Daniels for four long years, his loved one presumes he is dead. Needless to say, everyone is shocked by his sudden return. After spending time with him, some people soon notice that Ethan is not the same man who vanished all those years ago. After witnessing the gruesome death of his adopted sister, Naira, he wants one thing-revenge. He returns home to take out the man who is ultimately responsible for her death. However, once he reunites with Katrina, the girl he has loved since childhood, his desire for revenge begins to waver. As he falls more in love with Katrina each day, Ethan must decide what is more important-his love for her or his thirst for vengeance. <br /><br />This is a really good read filled with danger and suspense. The story progresses at the perfect pace, and all of the characters (even the secondary ones) are well developed. While it does end in a cliffhanger, I did see on one of the other reviews for this book that a sequel is in the works. I sure hope that is the case as I would love to know how Ethan's story plays out!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="8203114041006103768" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="J.A. Ironside" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15975161-j-a-ironside"><img alt="J.A. Ironside" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454955023p2/15975161.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1538549296?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J.A. Ironside" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J.A. Ironside" href="/user/show/15975161-j-a-ironside">J.A. Ironside</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22916648-dark-guardian">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1538549296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3151564279748728665">This is not my usual fare when chosing a book. All too often I find the male protagonist in these kinds of tales of self discovery and redemption difficult to access and the female characters, flimsy. Not so here. Habib has created a sympathetic protagonist who takes us on a compelling journey from would be anti-hero to believable good guy. Ethan starts the story driven by the desire for revenge. It was refreshing watching him gradually relinquish his hold on the need for personal satisfaction a</span>
  <span id="freeText3151564279748728665" style="display:none">This is not my usual fare when chosing a book. All too often I find the male protagonist in these kinds of tales of self discovery and redemption difficult to access and the female characters, flimsy. Not so here. Habib has created a sympathetic protagonist who takes us on a compelling journey from would be anti-hero to believable good guy. Ethan starts the story driven by the desire for revenge. It was refreshing watching him gradually relinquish his hold on the need for personal satisfaction and persue love instead. Too often the female lead has to pretzel herself into a shape that fits in with the male MC's myopic drive to get even. All the characters were well rounded, the story had a good pace with plenty to keep me interested and the action sequences were convincing. Four well deserved stars. I really enjoyed this.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3151564279748728665" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13311391807005320262" style="display:none">5 stars. Not a bad first novel, but I think the later books are better in this series. Probably because the author continued to mature in his craft. The story is a little bit more complicated here, with some extra characters. The story is written in chapters with little and big cliffhangers at the end of each one that moves the reader forward. The spoken dialogue is used to move the plot forward. The protagonist, Ethan Daniels, is similar to a Batman or Punisher type hero or anti-hero. The actions scenes are well done and engaging (and bloody). </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2294979108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8866294451740830235">I really enjoyed this book and can’t wait to read the next two books in the series. Again I love the layout of this authors book the size and that the pages are white I really enjoy as they are easily read. I know for most readers out there this wouldn’t be a feature they talk about but for people that don’t read often I think it helps. The story line was brilliant and the best bit for my reading nature is I didn’t guess what was going to happen next I read a lot of books and find I can predict </span>
  <span id="freeText8866294451740830235" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this book and can’t wait to read the next two books in the series. Again I love the layout of this authors book the size and that the pages are white I really enjoy as they are easily read. I know for most readers out there this wouldn’t be a feature they talk about but for people that don’t read often I think it helps. The story line was brilliant and the best bit for my reading nature is I didn’t guess what was going to happen next I read a lot of books and find I can predict what’s going to happen next. The story follows Ethan on his quest to avenge the death of his adoptive sister who was murdered by a gang. Ethan tracks them down and then starts to get information from people to get to the top man which is never easy. But like most story’s he is of course side tracked by the girl he grew up with and is now falling in love with. This amazing side part of the story is wonderful and I can’t wait to see were the second book takes us. Great read. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8866294451740830235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('o5kf88gbi0OxrIrdOfAmNEo2UnaNOip4i3RR9U7CNy5auAwr34Se5hXsFrI6kLinerfbrXmVfUrqmV8uEOtQ2g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HLoIiHGoPX4ayKgFkpB3H0UDBgHvi/u4YQLwTd2YEYjlmxtQZjco276INGqR8OmMdYKP2hskrIoA7/6Wg7F2fA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
